### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Forbidden_Words.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 5909 bytes, 146 lines**
# 🚫 MVQUEEN — Forbidden Words & Phrases

---

## Why This Document Exists

Words carry energy. The wrong word in MVQUEEN copy — no matter how good the surrounding content is — breaks the atmosphere.

This document exists to protect the brand's voice from the language patterns that make luxury brands sound cheap, generic, or out of alignment with their values.

Every person and AI system producing MVQUEEN content must review this list before publishing.

---

## Tier 1 — Never Use (Hard Prohibition)

These words and phrases are incompatible with MVQUEEN brand identity. They signal cheap, aggressive, or generic marketing and must never appear in customer-facing content.

| Word / Phrase | Why Forbidden |
|--------------|--------------|
| BOGO / Buy One Get One | Discount retailer energy |
| Flash sale | Desperate urgency, contradicts luxury |
| Limited time offer! | Manufactured panic, aggressive |
| Don't miss out! | Fear-based, pressure marketing |
| Act fast! | Pushy, unbecoming |
| Hurry! | Same as above |
| Slay | Overused, performative |
| Boss babe | Dated, contradicts brand voice |
| Girlboss | Same as above |
| Hustle | Contradicts softness philosophy |
| Grind | Same as above |
| Literally (in brand copy) | Too casual, filler word |
| Obsessed (as headline) | Overused, meaningless |
| You NEED this | Pressure-based |
| Game changer | Marketing cliché, hollow |
| Life changing | Overused, unsubstantiated |
| Amazing | Generic, no specificity |
| Incredible | Same as above |
| Stunning | Overused in beauty/fashion |
| Iconic (without context) | Hollow without earned meaning |
| Synergy | Corporate filler |
| Leverage (in brand copy) | Jargon |
| Disrupt / Disrupting | Tech startup language, off-brand |
| Empower (overused) | Has lost meaning through overuse |
| Fierce | Contradicts softness and calm |
| Baddie | Not aligned with brand identity |
| Bestie (in brand copy) | Too casual for luxury positioning |
| Slaying the game | Multiple violations |
| It's giving | Trend-dependent, fleeting |
| No cap | Same |
| Lowkey / Highkey | Same |

---

## Tier 2 — Use With Extreme Caution

These words are not forbidden but are so overused in beauty/fashion marketing that they require a specific, earned context to carry weight. If used, they must be supported by real substance.

| Word / Phrase | Caution |
|--------------|---------|
| Luxury | Overused — only use when describing a specific feeling or experience, not as a generic label |
| Elevated | Common — pair with specific sensory detail |
| Exclusive | Needs to mean something real, not just signaling |
| Premium | Generic — replace with specific quality descriptor |
| Empowered / Empowering | Has lost specificity — describe the actual feeling instead |
| Authentic | Overused — show authenticity, don't label it |
| Intentional | Used well in doctrine, but can become filler in copy |
| Emotional (as prefix) | Brand philosophy uses this well, but copy overuse dilutes it |
| Feminine | Use precisely — don't use as a vague adjective |
| Self-care | Overused category term — describe the specific ritual instead |
| Glow | Beauty cliché — use only with specific sensory context |
| Radiant | Same as glow |
| Transform / Transformation | Powerful but requires a real before/after to earn it |
| Ritual | Used correctly in brand voice but can become a filler word |
| Journey | Overused, vague |
| Community | Use only when describing a real community interaction |

---

## Tier 3 — Never Use in Headlines or Hero Copy

These are acceptable in body copy with context but must never lead a headline, subject line, or primary hook — they are too weak to carry the opening moment.

- *Good* (as in "good products")
- *Nice*
- *Great*
- *Wonderful*
- *Perfect*
- *Beautiful* (alone, without supporting context)
- *Special*
- *Unique* (without specificity)
- *Quality* (without specificity)
- *Affordable luxury* (contradicts brand positioning)

---

## Punctuation & Formatting Prohibitions

| Pattern | Why Forbidden |
|---------|--------------|
| Multiple exclamation marks!!! | Desperate energy |
| ALL CAPS WORDS in body copy | Aggressive, shouting |
| 🛍️🔥💯 (transactional emojis) | Contradicts luxury positioning |
| "Click here" | Lazy, no brand voice |
| Ellipsis overuse... | Amateur writing pattern |
| "I mean..." in brand copy | Too casual for any format |
| Sentence fragments used as filler | Only acceptable as intentional stylistic choice |

---

## Words We Replace

| Instead of... | Use... |
|--------------|--------|
| Amazing | Extraordinary / Remarkable / [Specific descriptor] |
| Luxury (generic) | [Describe the specific feeling of luxury] |
| Empowering | Restoring / Honoring / Elevating |
| Self-care | Ritual / Practice / Intention |
| Beautiful (alone) | [Describe what makes it beautiful specifically] |
| Game changer | [Describe the specific change it creates] |
| Obsessed | In love with / Can't put down / Returns to every day |
| Stunning | [Describe what creates the impact] |
| Good vibes | [Describe the specific atmosphere] |
| Fierce | Confident / Grounded / Present |
| Boss | Intentional / Decisive / In her power |

---

## AI Content Review Checklist

Before any AI-generated content is published, scan for:

```
□ Any Tier 1 words present? → Remove and replace
□ Any Tier 2 words used without specific context? → Revise
□ Any Tier 3 words in headlines? → Replace with stronger language
□ Multiple exclamation marks? → Remove
□ ALL CAPS in body copy? → Remove
□ Generic CTAs (Shop Now, Buy Now)? → Replace with CTA library options
□ Overuse of "emotionally" as a prefix? → Rewrite naturally
□ Any language that sounds like another brand? → Rewrite as MVQUEEN
```

---
*MVQUEEN Forbidden Words System — Operational Document*
*Review quarterly — language evolves and new clichés emerge.*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Voice_Consistency_Rules.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 5596 bytes, 121 lines**
# 👑 MVQUEEN — Voice Consistency Rules
### The Quick-Reference Card

---

## What This File Is

This is not the full tone guide. That lives in Tone_Guide.md.
This is the card you check *before you publish* anything.
One page. Every rule that matters. No philosophy — just mechanics.

Print it. Pin it. Feed it to every AI prompt. Run every piece of copy through it before it goes live.

---

## THE 10 LAWS

**LAW 01 — Lead with feeling, follow with fact.**
The customer should feel something in the first sentence. What the product *does* comes after what it *feels like.*
> ❌ "Our new fragrance contains notes of jasmine and sandalwood."
> ✅ "The kind of scent that makes you stand differently. Jasmine, sandalwood, and something that feels like arriving."

---

**LAW 02 — Write in motion, not in lists.**
MVQUEEN copy moves. It doesn't enumerate. Bullet points belong in internal documents — not in customer-facing language unless functionally necessary (ingredients, sizing, care instructions).
> ❌ "This serum is: hydrating, brightening, and lightweight."
> ✅ "Lightweight enough to disappear into skin. Hydrating enough to change what your skin says about you."

---

**LAW 03 — Never use a word you wouldn't say out loud in this brand's voice.**
Read every line aloud. If it sounds like a press release, a wellness blog, or a discount ad — rewrite it.

---

**LAW 04 — Specificity over adjectives.**
Vague luxury words (beautiful, luxurious, exquisite) tell. Specific sensory detail shows.
> ❌ "Luxurious packaging you'll love."
> ✅ "Matte-finish box. Weighted closure. The kind of packaging that makes throwing it away feel wrong."

---

**LAW 05 — Short sentences are power. Use them.**
A three-word sentence hits harder than a ten-word one when placed correctly. Don't fear the period.
> "She already knows her worth. MVQUEEN just makes it visible."

---

**LAW 06 — She is never talked down to. She is spoken with.**
The MVQUEEN customer is intelligent, self-aware, and emotionally sharp. Copy that over-explains or over-reassures sounds condescending. Trust her.
> ❌ "We know you're busy, so we made this easy."
> ✅ "Everything you need. Nothing that wastes your time."

---

**LAW 07 — Emotional words must earn their placement.**
"Emotional," "elevated," "intentional," "immersive" — each of these is allowed a maximum of twice per 300 words. When you feel yourself defaulting to them, find the specific image or sensation behind the word and write that instead.

---

**LAW 08 — Aspiration does not exclude. It invites.**
MVQUEEN copy should make a woman feel like she already belongs in this world — not that she's working toward being worthy of it. The door is open. She's already inside.
> ❌ "Step into luxury."
> ✅ "This is what you already deserve."

---

**LAW 09 — Miss.Princess gets a different filter.**
When writing for Miss.Princess: warmer, softer, more playful, more trend-aware. Shorter sentences. More energy. But the same quality bar. Miss.Princess is not a discounted version of MVQUEEN — she is a different register of the same standard.

---

**LAW 10 — If you can cut it and the sentence still works, cut it.**
MVQUEEN copy is not long. It is *weighted.* The difference between a brand that sounds luxurious and one that sounds like it's trying to — is that the first one knows when to stop.

---

## PLATFORM TONE CALIBRATION

| Platform | Energy | Sentence Length | Emoji Use |
|---|---|---|---|
| Website hero | Cinematic, atmospheric | Short — medium | None |
| Product page | Sensory, confident | Medium | None or rare |
| Email subject | Intriguing, warm | Very short | Rare |
| Email body | Personal, elegant | Medium | None |
| Instagram caption | Immersive, expressive | Variable — poetic allowed | 1 max |
| TikTok / Reels hook | Direct, magnetic | Very short, punchy | Optional |
| Pinterest | Atmospheric, aspirational | Short | None |
| SMS | Warm, direct | Very short | 1 max |
| Customer support | Calm, human, warm | Conversational | None |
| Miss.Princess social | Playful, soft, energetic | Short, rhythmic | 2–3 max |

---

## VOICE FAILS — RECOGNIZE & FIX

| If it sounds like this... | It's failing because... | Fix it by... |
|---|---|---|
| A wellness influencer | Too much "allow yourself" energy | Remove the permission — she doesn't need it |
| A discount retailer | Urgency, deal language, price focus | Lead with experience, not price |
| A corporate press release | Passive voice, formal nouns, no feeling | Rewrite in active voice with sensory detail |
| A self-help account | Clichés, empty affirmations | Replace with specific, earned statements |
| A different luxury brand | Borrowed tone, generic adjectives | Go back to MVQUEEN vocabulary — what does *this* brand specifically feel like? |
| A brand from 2019 | Expired slang, boss babe language | Run through Forbidden_Words.md |

---

## THE FINAL CHECK — 3 QUESTIONS BEFORE PUBLISHING

Before any piece of content goes live, answer these three questions honestly:

1. **Does it sound like MVQUEEN — specifically?** Not like a beautiful brand. Like *this* brand.
2. **Does it make her feel something?** If you can read it and feel nothing, rewrite it.
3. **Would it survive the Forbidden Words audit?** Run it through the list.

If all three answers are yes — publish.

---

*This file is the voice quick-reference. It pairs with Tone_Guide.md (full philosophy), Writing_Rules.md (mechanics), and Forbidden_Words.md (vocabulary law). Together these four files govern everything MVQUEEN writes.*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Writing_Rules.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 9786 bytes, 222 lines**
# 👑 MVQUEEN — Writing Rules
### The Craft Manual

---

## What This File Governs

Voice is *what* MVQUEEN sounds like.
Writing Rules are *how* that voice gets built at the sentence level.

This file is for anyone who writes for MVQUEEN — humans and AI systems alike. It covers sentence mechanics, structure, rhythm, formatting, and the specific craft decisions that separate MVQUEEN copy from everything else in the market.

Follow these rules and the voice will hold.
Ignore them and it won't matter how good your intentions were.

---

## PART 1 — SENTENCE MECHANICS

### Rule 01 — Active Voice. Always.
Passive voice removes the brand from the experience. MVQUEEN does not happen *to* women. It happens *with* them and *for* them.

> ❌ "This serum was formulated to restore radiance."
> ✅ "This serum restores radiance — and reminds skin what it's capable of."

Passive voice is only permitted in legal disclaimers and ingredient disclosures.

---

### Rule 02 — Vary Sentence Length Deliberately
Short sentences create impact. Medium sentences carry information. Long sentences create rhythm and immersion. MVQUEEN copy uses all three — never one at the expense of the others.

The pattern that works most reliably:
> Long sentence that creates atmosphere. Short sentence that lands the point. Medium sentence that extends it naturally.

Example:
> "Getting dressed for yourself — not for anyone watching — is one of the most quietly powerful things a woman can do. MVQUEEN was made for that moment. The one that exists before the world gets to see it."

---

### Rule 03 — The Em Dash Is Your Best Structural Tool
The em dash (—) creates a natural pause, adds a layer of meaning, and gives copy a rhythmic sophistication that commas and colons don't.

> "The kind of confidence that arrives quietly — and stays."
> "Not a fragrance. An atmosphere — one you carry with you."

Use it. Don't overuse it. Maximum two em dashes per paragraph.

---

### Rule 04 — The Line Break Is Not Decoration
In MVQUEEN copy — especially in social captions, product descriptions, and campaign copy — line breaks are punctuation. They create visual breathing room and control how the reader moves through the copy.

> "She doesn't wait for permission.
> She doesn't perform confidence.
> She simply already knows."

A line break tells the reader: *pause here. Let this land.*

Do not use line breaks in email body copy or website paragraphs — only in display copy and social.

---

### Rule 05 — Periods Inside Thought Fragments Are Intentional
MVQUEEN copy sometimes uses fragment sentences — incomplete grammatically, complete emotionally. This is intentional style, not an error.

> "For the woman who already knows. For the one who's still learning. For both."

Fragments work when they accumulate. They fail when they replace complete thought. Use them for emotional punctuation, not as a substitute for writing actual sentences.

---

### Rule 06 — Eliminate Filler Qualifiers
These words make copy softer in the wrong way — they dilute confidence without adding warmth:

Remove: *very, really, quite, just, a bit, somewhat, kind of, sort of, a little, actually, truly, truly truly*

> ❌ "This is actually a really beautiful fragrance."
> ✅ "This fragrance does what it says. Beautifully."

---

### Rule 07 — Numbers in Copy
- Spell out numbers one through nine: *three, seven, nine*
- Use numerals for 10 and above: *12, 45, 100*
- Always use numerals for percentages, measurements, and prices: *30ml, $68, 15%*
- Times of day: *7 AM, noon, 11 PM* — not "seven in the morning"

---

## PART 2 — STRUCTURE

### Rule 08 — Every Product Description Has Three Jobs
In this order:
1. **Create desire** — before the product is named, she should want the feeling it delivers
2. **Describe the product** — what it is, what it contains, what it does
3. **Confirm the identity** — remind her why it belongs in her world specifically

> "Getting ready shouldn't feel like preparation. It should feel like ritual. [PRODUCT NAME] is a [what it is] that [what it does] — [sensory detail]. [Key ingredient/feature]. Made for the woman who treats self-care as a standard, not a reward."

---

### Rule 09 — Email Copy Structure
Every MVQUEEN email follows this emotional arc regardless of its purpose:

1. **Subject line** — creates intrigue or warmth, never urgency or discounting
2. **Opening line** — emotional hook; she should feel something before she reads anything
3. **Body** — product/offer/story told through experience, not announcement
4. **CTA** — one. Single. Not three buttons competing for attention.
5. **Sign-off** — warm, personal, on-brand. Never "The MVQUEEN Team." Sign as *MVQUEEN* or from a named brand voice.

---

### Rule 10 — Social Caption Structure
Instagram and long-form social captions follow this structure:

1. **Hook (line 1)** — stops the scroll; emotional, direct, or atmospheric
2. **Body (2–5 lines)** — develops the idea, story, or product context
3. **Landing line** — the line that stays with her after she scrolls away
4. **CTA (optional)** — gentle, not aggressive; one action only
5. **Hashtags** — below a line break, never embedded in the caption body

---

### Rule 11 — Campaign Copy Structure
For launches, collections, and seasonal campaigns:

1. **Campaign headline** — the single most important line; tested before anything else
2. **Sub-headline** — extends the headline's emotional direction
3. **Body copy** — 2–4 sentences maximum; atmospheric, not informational
4. **Product CTA** — clean, single-focus
5. **Visual relationship** — the copy must *add* to the visual, never explain it

If the image already says something, the copy says something *else* — something deeper.

---

## PART 3 — FORMATTING RULES

### Rule 12 — Capitalization
- Brand name: always **MVQUEEN** — all caps, no space
- Sister brand: always **Miss.Princess** — capital M, capital P, period between
- Product names: Title Case
- Collection names: Title Case
- Headlines: Title Case for formal documents; Sentence case for conversational copy
- Do not capitalize common nouns for emphasis (*Beauty, Confidence, Woman*) — this pattern reads as generic brand speak

---

### Rule 13 — Punctuation Hierarchy in Copy
- **Period** — full stop, maximum confidence
- **Em dash (—)** — layered meaning, rhythmic pause
- **Ellipsis (...)** — use *only* to create intentional suspension; not as lazy punctuation
- **Exclamation marks** — avoid in MVQUEEN copy. Miss.Princess may use one per caption maximum.
- **Question marks** — use sparingly in body copy; effective in subject lines and hooks
- **Ampersand (&)** — permitted in product names and collection names only; not in body copy
- **Quotation marks** — for actual quotes only; not for emphasis or irony

---

### Rule 14 — Bold and Italic Use
- **Bold** — for critical product information (key ingredient, size, key claim) and document navigation only; never for emotional emphasis in customer copy
- *Italic* — for product names referenced within copy, foreign words, and titles; not for emotional emphasis
- Do not bold or italicize words in social captions or email body copy for stylistic effect — the writing should create emphasis, not the formatting

---

### Rule 15 — Header Hierarchy in Documents
For internal OS documents:
- `# H1` — document title only (one per document)
- `## H2` — major sections
- `### H3` — subsections
- `#### H4` — only if absolutely necessary; if you're at H4, consider restructuring

For customer-facing copy (product pages, website):
- No visible H tags in the final experience — use only within CMS structure

---

## PART 4 — MVQUEEN-SPECIFIC STYLE DECISIONS

### Rule 16 — How to Introduce the Brand Name
In copy, MVQUEEN is referred to as:
- **MVQUEEN** (primary)
- **the brand** (in longer editorial pieces, after first use)
- Never as "we" in third-person contexts (choose either first or third person and commit)
- Never as "MVQUEEN brand" — redundant

---

### Rule 17 — How to Reference Miss.Princess
- Always **Miss.Princess** — never "Miss Princess" (no period = wrong), never "miss.princess" (lowercase = wrong)
- In MVQUEEN-primary copy, Miss.Princess is introduced as: *"our sister brand, Miss.Princess"*
- In Miss.Princess-primary copy, she stands alone — no need to reference MVQUEEN unless brand relationship is the editorial focus
- The two brands are **sister brands**, not sub-brands or lines. Miss.Princess is a peer, not a product category.

---

### Rule 18 — How to Write About the Customer
- She is **she** — never "they" in brand copy (singular they is for accessibility/legal contexts)
- She is never addressed as "girl" in MVQUEEN copy (Miss.Princess may use it sparingly)
- She is never a demographic label (*millennials, Gen Z, women 25–35*) in customer-facing copy
- She is described by her *emotional state and aspirations*, not her age or income

> ❌ "For women aged 25–45 who love fashion."
> ✅ "For the woman who treats getting dressed as a form of self-expression."

---

### Rule 19 — The Test Before You Ship

Read the copy out loud. Then ask:
- Does it sound like a real person who loves this brand wrote this?
- Does it make her feel something before it tells her anything?
- Is there a single word on the Forbidden Words list?
- Is every sentence doing work — or is any sentence just taking up space?

If you can answer yes, yes, no, yes — it ships.

---

*This file governs the mechanics of how MVQUEEN writes. Pair with Voice_Consistency_Rules.md for the quick-reference card, Tone_Guide.md for voice philosophy, and Forbidden_Words.md for vocabulary law.*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/CTA_Library.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 4698 bytes, 190 lines**
# 👑 MVQUEEN — CTA Library

---

## CTA Philosophy

MVQUEEN CTAs feel like invitations — not commands.

The difference between a CTA that converts and one that repels
is the difference between *"Buy Now"* and *"She deserves this."*

Every CTA should make her feel like she's choosing something for herself —
not being pushed toward a transaction.

**The rule:** Every CTA ends a feeling — it does not start a sale.

---

## CTA Categories

---

### Product CTAs

**Standard purchase:**
- *She's been waiting.* → Shop Now
- *Make it yours.*
- *Start your ritual.*
- *It was made for this.*
- *Add it to your world.*
- *Bring her home.*
- *Claim yours.*
- *It's time.*

**Limited / launch:**
- *She won't wait long.*
- *First access — yours now.*
- *Before she's gone.*
- *While she's still here.*
- *Don't let her slip.*

**Bundle / value:**
- *Build your ritual.*
- *The full experience.*
- *Everything she needs.*
- *Complete the set.*

---

### Email CTAs

**Button copy (replaces generic "Shop Now"):**
- *Yes, I want this.*
- *Take me there.*
- *Show me more.*
- *I'm ready.*
- *Let's go.*
- *She's mine.*
- *Discover [Product Name].*
- *Enter her world.*

**End-of-email CTA lines (before button):**
- *She was made for you. The only question is when.*
- *This is your invitation.*
- *You've been thinking about it. This is the sign.*
- *Luxury shouldn't wait. Neither should you.*
- *She's here. You just have to say yes.*

---

### Social CTAs

**Caption closing lines:**
- *Link in bio — she's waiting.*
- *Tap the link. Start the ritual.*
- *She's in the link. Go find her.*
- *Your ritual is one tap away.*
- *Tell me in the comments — would you?*
- *Save this for when you're ready.*
- *Which one is yours? Drop it below.*
- *Tag someone who deserves this.*
- *Share this with her.*

**Story CTAs:**
- *Swipe up. She's ready.*
- *Tap to meet her.*
- *This is for you. Tap.*
- *The link lives here.*

---

### Ad CTAs

**Meta ad CTA buttons (beyond default):**
- Shop Now → *Start Your Ritual*
- Learn More → *Discover MVQUEEN*
- Sign Up → *Join the World*
- Get Offer → *Claim Yours*

**Ad copy closing lines:**
- *Your softness deserves this. Shop MVQUEEN.*
- *She's been waiting. So have you.*
- *Luxury made for women like you. Shop now.*
- *This is the one. You already know it.*

---

### Email Subject Line CTAs (curiosity-driven)

- *Something we made for you.*
- *She's finally here.*
- *You asked. We listened.*
- *This one's personal.*
- *We saved you one.*
- *For the version of you who's ready.*
- *A gift — inside.*
- *She won't last long.*
- *First look. Just for you.*
- *We need to tell you something.*

---

### SMS CTAs

Full SMS messages that ARE the CTA:
- *Your MVQUEEN order is on its way. She was packed with intention. 🤍*
- *Something new just arrived — and it has your name on it. [LINK]*
- *You left something behind. She's still here waiting. [LINK]*
- *Early access — just for you. New arrivals live now. [LINK]*
- *Your ritual is incomplete. Meet the missing piece. [LINK]*

---

### Community / UGC CTAs

- *Show us your MVQUEEN moment. Tag us — we're watching.*
- *How does she make you feel? Tell us in the comments.*
- *Share your ritual. #MVQUEEN*
- *We want to see her in your world. Tag @mvqueen.*
- *Your review means everything to us — and to women like you.*

---

## CTA Formulas

### Formula 01 — The Identity CTA
Connect the action to who she is.
`[Action] + [identity statement]`

*Shop the ritual. You've earned this version of yourself.*
*Claim yours. Soft women deserve soft things.*

### Formula 02 — The Permission CTA
Give her permission to act.
`You're allowed to [desire]. [Action].`

*You're allowed to want this. Shop now.*
*You deserve the ritual. Start here.*

### Formula 03 — The Urgency-Without-Pressure CTA
Create desire without manufactured panic.
`[Soft scarcity] + [invitation]`

*She won't be here forever. Make her yours.*
*Limited first batch — yours while she lasts.*

### Formula 04 — The Curiosity CTA
Make her want to know more.
`[Question or tease] → [Action]`

*Wondering what the ritual feels like? Tap to find out.*
*She's been our best-kept secret. Until now. Shop.*

---

## CTAs We Never Use

| Avoid | Why |
|-------|-----|
| SHOP NOW (all caps) | Aggressive, demand-based |
| BUY NOW | Transactional, no feeling |
| LIMITED TIME OFFER!!! | Manufactured panic |
| Don't miss out! | Pressure-based, not invitation |
| Act fast! | Desperate energy |
| Click here | Generic, no brand voice |
| Add to cart | Functional only, no emotional context |

---
*MVQUEEN CTA Library — Operational Document*
*Add new high-performing CTAs as they are tested and proven.*

# Example_Copy.md
**Location:** `06_Tone_And_Voice/Example_Copy.md`
**Doctrine Anchor:** `00_Doctrine/README.md` — Quiet Confidence, Warm Luxury, Feminine Precision
**Authority:** Reference library of approved brand copy across all formats and channels

---

## 01 — Purpose

This file is a living reference. Every example here passed the brand voice test and can be used as a template, a benchmark, or a prompt seed for new copy.

Writers, designers, and AI agents use this file to calibrate tone before producing new content. When in doubt about whether something sounds right — come here first.

---

## 02 — Homepage Copy

### Hero Headlines
```
She already knows what she wants.
We just made it easier to find.
```
```
Dressed for the life she's building.
```
```
Not trend-chasing. Intentional dressing.
```
```
The edit for women who know their worth.
```
```
Quality that speaks before she does.
```

### Hero Subheadlines
```
MvQueen is a curated fashion destination built for women
who dress with intention. No noise. Just the pieces that work.
```
```
Every piece selected for fit, finish, and staying power.
Because your wardrobe should work as hard as you do.
```

### Section Intros
```
The Collection
New pieces. Intentional picks. Nothing filler.
```
```
Built for her.
Not for the trend cycle. Not for the algorithm.
For the woman who already knows who she is.
```

---

## 03 — Product Description Examples

### Bodysuit
```
The kind of piece that does the work for you.
Clean lines, secure fit, no adjusting required.
Wear it under high-waist trousers or let it lead.
Either way — effortless is the only outcome.
```

### Midi Dress
```
Not trying to be a statement. Just quietly is one.
The [Product Name] in [color] — fitted through the waist,
relaxed from the hip. The fabric holds its shape.
So does she.
```

### Co-ord Set
```
Because matching shouldn't take effort.
The [Set Name] was designed as a complete look —
but the pieces go just as well apart.
Style it together or split it. Both answers are right.
```

### Accessories
```
The finishing detail.
Not the loudest thing in the room — the most considered.
[Product Name] in [material]. Made to last the full day
and look better for it.
```

---

## 04 — Email Copy Examples

### Welcome Email — Subject Line Options
```
Welcome to MvQueen. You're in the right place.
Your edit starts here.
The pieces you've been looking for. They're here.
```

### Welcome Email — Body
```
Hi [First Name],

You made it here for a reason.

MvQueen is built for women who dress with intention —
not to keep up, but to stand out in the quietest,
most confident way possible.

Everything in this store was chosen with you in mind.
Not the trend-chaser. The woman who already knows
what works for her and just needs a brand that does too.

Start with the new arrivals. Or take your time.
Either way, we're glad you're here.

— The MvQueen Edit
```

### Abandoned Cart Email — Subject Lines
```
Still thinking about it?
Your bag is waiting.
It's still yours — for now.
```

### Abandoned Cart — Body
```
Hi [First Name],

You left something behind.

[Product Name] is still in your bag —
and still available. But these go fast.

If you have questions about fit, sizing, or styling,
reply to this email. We're here.

Otherwise — it's one click away.

[CTA: Complete Your Order]
```

### New Arrival Email — Subject Lines
```
New in: the pieces worth knowing about.
The edit just got better.
Fresh drop. No filler.
```

### Sale Email — Subject Lines
```
Selected pieces. Reduced prices. Still the same standard.
The sale edit is live.
Worth every penny — now more so.
```

---

## 05 — Social Media Caption Examples

### Product Feature (Instagram)
```
The [Product Name].
Clean. Precise. Built to be worn, not saved for later.

Available now — link in bio.
```

### Lifestyle / Brand Moment
```
She's not getting dressed for anyone else.
That's the whole point.
```

### New Arrival
```
Just landed: [Product Name] in [color/style].
The kind of piece that earns its space in the wardrobe.

Link in bio.
```

### Customer Feature / UGC Repost
```
When she styles it better than the lookbook.
[@handle] in the [Product Name].

Shop the look — link in bio.
```

### Behind the Brand
```
Every piece goes through the same filter:
Would we wear it? Would we keep it?
If the answer isn't immediate — it doesn't make the edit.
```

### Engagement Post
```
Tell us: which colorway goes in the wardrobe first?
[Option A] or [Option B].
```

---

## 06 — miss.queen Caption Examples

miss.queen captions carry more energy and speak to a slightly younger audience. Same precision, lighter touch.

```
Okay but this set though. 🖤
[Product Name] just dropped and it's giving everything.
Link in bio.
```
```
New drop just landed and we are NOT calm.
[Product Name] — available now.
```
```
Your next favorite outfit is officially in the building.
Shop the [Collection Name] — link in bio.
```

---

## 07 — SMS Copy Examples

| Occasion | Copy |
|---|---|
| New arrival | New drop just landed. [Product Name] — shop now: [link] |
| Flash sale | 24-hour sale is live. Selected pieces only: [link] |
| Back in stock | It's back. [Product Name] in [color] — get it before it goes again: [link] |
| Order shipped | Your MvQueen order is on its way. Track it here: [link] |
| Abandoned cart | Still thinking? Your bag is saved: [link] |

## 08 — Ad Copy Examples

### Meta / Instagram Ad — Short Form
```
Primary text:
She doesn't follow trends. She sets her own standard.
MvQueen — fashion for women who dress with intention.

Headline: Shop the Edit
CTA: Shop Now
```

### Meta / Instagram Ad — Long Form
```
Primary text:
If you've been looking for a brand that gets it —
this is it.

MvQueen is built around one idea:
you already know who you are. You just need
pieces that match that energy.

No fast fashion. No trend chasing.
Just a carefully curated edit that works
as hard as you do.

New arrivals are in. Take a look.

Headline: The MvQueen Edit — Shop Now
```

### Retargeting Ad
```
You looked. We noticed.
[Product Name] is still available — but not forever.

Headline: Still Interested?
CTA: Get Yours
```

## 09 — Brand Voice Comparison Table

Use this to self-check copy before publishing.

| Off-Brand | On-Brand |
|---|---|
| "Amazing styles you'll love!" | "Pieces worth keeping." |
| "Shop our huge collection NOW!!!" | "Shop the Edit." |
| "Don't miss out on this deal!" | "The sale is live. Selected pieces only." |
| "We're so excited to share this!" | "New in. Worth a look." |
| "Our customers absolutely love this product!" | "This one earns its place in the wardrobe." |
| "Hurry — selling out fast!" | "These go quickly. Yours while it lasts." |
| "This gorgeous dress is perfect for any occasion!" | "Dressed down or up. Either way, it works." |

### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Product_Description_Voice.md
**STATUS: POPULATED — 8061 bytes, 242 lines**
# Product_Description_Voice.md
**Location:** `06_Tone_And_Voice/Product_Description_Voice.md`
**Doctrine Anchor:** `00_Doctrine/README.md` — Quiet Confidence, Warm Luxury, Feminine Precision
**Authority:** Writing standard for all MvQueen and miss.queen product descriptions

---

## 01 — Philosophy

A product description is not a spec sheet. It is the moment the customer decides whether she trusts us.

She's already looking at the image. She already likes what she sees. The description's job is to close the gap between *wanting it* and *buying it* — not by pushing, but by confirming what she already feels.

MvQueen descriptions are written for a woman who is decisive. She does not need six paragraphs. She needs precise detail, delivered with confidence.

**The test for every description:**
> *Does this make her feel certain — about the product and about herself for choosing it?*

---

## 02 — Description Architecture

Every product description follows this structure. Not every section needs multiple sentences — some need one. Precision over padding.

```
[Opening Hook]       — 1–2 lines. Feeling first. Not features first.
[What It Is]         — What the product actually is and does.
[How It Wears]       — Fit, feel, movement. What the body experiences.
[Styling Direction]  — 1–2 ways to wear it. Not exhaustive — curated.
[Product Details]    — Bullet list: material, fit type, sizing notes, care.
```

---

## 03 — Section-by-Section Guide

### Opening Hook
Lead with the feeling or the outcome — not the product name or a feature.

| ❌ Off-Brand | ✅ On-Brand |
|---|---|
| "This beautiful dress features..." | "The kind of dress that earns compliments without asking for them." |
| "Introducing our new bodysuit!" | "Does the work so she doesn't have to." |
| "A must-have for every wardrobe!" | "Not a trend. A decision." |
| "This stunning co-ord set is perfect..." | "Together or apart. Both answers are right." |

The hook is 1–2 lines maximum. It sets the tone. Then get to the product.

---

### What It Is
State the product clearly. No fluff. Include the key design feature that makes it worth buying.

```
The [Product Name] is a [silhouette/category] cut from [fabric] with [defining feature].
```

Examples:
```
The Ava Midi is a fitted-waist dress cut from stretch crepe with a subtle flare from the knee.
The Reign Bodysuit is a scoop-neck seamless bodysuit designed to lay flat under anything.
The Court Set is a tailored co-ord in woven linen — structured top, wide-leg trouser.
```

---

### How It Wears
Describe the physical experience. Fit, movement, structure, comfort. This is where she imagines herself in it.

Focus on:
- How it fits (body-skimming, relaxed, structured, etc.)
- What the fabric does (holds shape, drapes, stretches, breathes)
- What makes it practical to actually wear

```
Fitted through the waist and hip, relaxed from mid-thigh. 
The fabric holds without pulling — no lining required.
```
```
The waistband sits high and stays there. No rolling, no adjusting.
```
```
Lightweight enough for all-day wear. Structured enough to carry itself.
```

---

### Styling Direction
Give her 1–2 specific directions. Not "style with anything!" — curated suggestions that reflect the brand's eye.

```
Wear with strappy heels and a clutch for evening.
Pair with white trainers and a blazer for the daytime version.
```
```
Style the set together for the full look.
Or wear the top with denim — both answers are right.
```

---

### Product Details (Bullet Format)
This section is functional. Keep it scannable.

```
- Fabric: 95% Polyester, 5% Elastane
- Fit: True to size — size up if between sizes
- Length: Midi (hits below knee on 5'6")
- Closure: Concealed back zip
- Care: Hand wash cold, lay flat to dry
- Model: Wearing size M, height 5'7"
```

Include only what's genuinely useful. Do not add bullets to pad length.

---

## 04 — Tone Calibration by Product Type

| Product Type | Tone | Key Focus |
|---|---|---|
| Bodysuits | Functional confidence | Fit precision, no-fuss wear |
| Dresses | Elevated, desire-building | Silhouette, occasion, feeling |
| Co-ord sets | Effortless, editorial | Versatility, the full look |
| Trousers / bottoms | Practical authority | Fit, movement, pairing |
| Tops | Direct, versatile | What it goes with, what it does |
| Accessories | Considered, finishing | The detail that completes |
| Occasionwear | Elevated, certain | The moment she's dressing for |

---

## 05 — Length Guide

| Product Category | Target Length | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| Core basics (bodysuit, simple top) | 60–80 words + bullets | Short. Confident. Done. |
| Dresses | 80–120 words + bullets | More styling context |
| Co-ords / sets | 80–120 words + bullets | Address both pieces |
| Occasionwear | 100–140 words + bullets | More atmosphere, more detail |
| Accessories | 40–60 words + bullets | Brief — product sells itself visually |

**Hard rule:** No description exceeds 150 words of prose. Details go in the bullet list.

---

## 06 — Words That Earn Their Place

Use these. They carry weight without overreaching.

| Word/Phrase | Why It Works |
|---|---|
| Intentional | Signals that the design was considered |
| Earns its place | Value language — not trend, not impulse |
| Works hard | Practical luxury |
| Precise | Feminine confidence |
| Holds | Physical reliability |
| Quietly | Understated excellence |
| Either way | Gives her control |
| Stays there | Practical trust |

---

## 07 — Words to Avoid

| Word / Phrase | Problem |
|---|---|
| Amazing / stunning / gorgeous | Generic — every brand says this |
| Perfect for any occasion | Lazy — be specific |
| Must-have | Pressure language — not brand voice |
| Luxurious | Overused — show it, don't say it |
| Flattering | Vague — describe the actual fit |
| Beautiful | Empty without specifics |
| Obsessed | Too casual for MvQueen (acceptable for miss.queen only) |
| Super soft / super comfortable | "Super" is filler |
| You'll love | Presumptuous |
| Don't miss | Urgency without basis |

---

## 08 — miss.queen Description Adjustments

miss.queen descriptions carry the same structure but with lighter energy. The hook can be more direct and fun. The language can be slightly more casual.

| Element | MvQueen | miss.queen |
|---|---|---|
| Hook tone | Composed, certain | Direct, energetic |
| Styling direction | Curated, editorial | Fun, immediate |
| Adjective range | Intentional, precise, composed | Clean, fresh, easy, fun |
| Length | Same | Same — precision still applies |

**miss.queen example:**
```
Your new favorite going-out top just arrived.

The [Product Name] fits close through the body with a slight stretch — 
enough to move, not enough to shift. Wear it tucked into a mini 
or let it sit at the hip with wide-leg trousers.

Either way, it works.

- Fabric: 92% Nylon, 8% Spandex
- Fit: Fitted — true to size
- Care: Machine wash cold
- Model: Wearing size S, height 5'5"
```

---

## 09 — Full Description Example (MvQueen)

**Product:** The Reign Midi Dress — Black

```
Not trying to be a statement. Just quietly is one.

The Reign Midi is a fitted-waist dress cut from stretch crepe — 
structured enough to hold its shape, soft enough to wear all day. 
It skims the body through the waist and hip before falling straight 
from the knee. Clean lines. No excess.

Wear it with pointed mules and a structured bag for evening. 
Or dress it back with white trainers — the silhouette carries both.

- Fabric: 96% Polyester, 4% Elastane
- Fit: Fitted — true to size, size up for more ease
- Length: Midi (below knee on 5'6")
- Closure: Concealed back zip
- Care: Hand wash cold, hang to dry
- Model: Wearing size M, height 5'7"
```

---

| Version | Date | Change |
|---|---|---|
| 1.0 | Phase 2 Build | Purpose-built — not extracted from Brand Bible |

*This file is used by all copywriters, VAs, and AI agents producing product descriptions. No exceptions.*

### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Hook_Systems.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 6546 bytes, 213 lines**
# 🪝 MVQUEEN — Hook Systems

---

## What Makes a Hook Work

A hook has one job: stop her mid-scroll and make her feel something in under 3 seconds.

Not inform. Not sell. **Feel.**

The best MVQUEEN hooks create a micro-moment of recognition —
she sees herself, her desire, or her problem reflected back at her
before she even realizes she stopped scrolling.

---

## The 12 MVQUEEN Hook Formulas

---

### Formula 01 — The Identity Mirror
Reflect who she already is or who she is becoming.
She stops because she sees herself.

**Structure:** `For the woman who ___`

**Examples:**
- *For the woman who treats softness like a discipline.*
- *For the woman who is done performing and ready to just live.*
- *For the woman building a life that feels as good as it looks.*
- *For the woman who romanticizes everything — and isn't sorry.*

---

### Formula 02 — The Quiet Disruption
Challenge a common belief without being aggressive.
She stops because something feels true that she never heard said out loud.

**Structure:** `[Common assumption] is a lie. / Nobody talks about ___`

**Examples:**
- *Luxury isn't supposed to feel intimidating.*
- *Softness is not something you grow out of.*
- *Nobody talks about how beauty should restore you — not exhaust you.*
- *Self-care wasn't supposed to become another thing to optimize.*

---

### Formula 03 — The Sensory Open
Drop her into a feeling before she knows what you're selling.
She stops because she wants to stay in the feeling.

**Structure:** `[Sensory moment] — [what it means]`

**Examples:**
- *The kind of morning where everything feels intentional.*
- *Skin so soft you forget to overthink.*
- *That feeling when your space finally matches who you're becoming.*
- *Slow mornings. Good products. Nothing to prove.*

---

### Formula 04 — The Honest Admission
Be real in a way other brands aren't.
She stops because it sounds human — not marketing.

**Structure:** `We made this because ___` / `Honestly, ___`

**Examples:**
- *We made this for the days when you need beauty to do the emotional heavy lifting.*
- *Honestly? Most luxury brands weren't built for women like you.*
- *We didn't create another skincare routine. We created a ritual.*

---

### Formula 05 — The Before State
Name exactly where she is right now.
She stops because she feels understood.

**Structure:** `If you've ever felt ___ / been tired of ___`

**Examples:**
- *If you've ever bought something beautiful and felt nothing.*
- *If you're tired of beauty routines that feel like chores.*
- *If you've been waiting for a brand that actually gets it.*
- *If "good enough" stopped being enough.*

---

### Formula 06 — The Transformation Tease
Show the after without giving away the how.
She stops because she wants to know more.

**Structure:** `What if ___ felt different?`

**Examples:**
- *What if your morning routine felt like the best part of your day?*
- *What if luxury actually felt like it was made for you?*
- *What if softness was something you could wear?*

---

### Formula 07 — The Specificity Hook
Be so specific she thinks you know her personally.
She stops because it's too accurate to ignore.

**Structure:** `[Very specific scenario she recognizes]`

**Examples:**
- *The candle. The silk pillowcase. The skincare you actually use.*
- *Not the "treat yourself" spiral. The intentional kind of self-care.*
- *The version of you that takes her time. She deserves better products.*

---

### Formula 08 — The Contrast Hook
Put two opposites next to each other.
She stops because the tension is interesting.

**Structure:** `[Contrast A] not [Contrast B]`

**Examples:**
- *Soft, not weak. Elevated, not unreachable.*
- *Made for real life — not a photoshoot.*
- *Luxury that feels lived-in, not staged.*
- *Feminine without the performance.*

---

### Formula 09 — The Permission Hook
Give her permission she didn't know she needed.
She stops because it feels like relief.

**Structure:** `You're allowed to ___`

**Examples:**
- *You're allowed to want things that feel beautiful.*
- *You're allowed to take up space softly.*
- *You're allowed to choose luxury without justifying it.*
- *You're allowed to romanticize your everyday life.*

---

### Formula 10 — The Number Hook
Use a specific number to signal value.
She stops because specificity implies expertise.

**Structure:** `[Number] things / ways / reasons`

**Examples:**
- *3 things in your routine that should feel like rituals, not tasks.*
- *The one product my shelf hasn't been without in 6 months.*
- *5 signs your self-care has become another performance.*

---

### Formula 11 — The Question Hook
Ask the question she's already asking herself.
She stops because she wants the answer.

**Structure:** `[Question she already has]`

**Examples:**
- *Why does skincare feel like a chore when it should feel like a ritual?*
- *What does luxury actually feel like when it's made for you?*
- *Is it possible to feel elevated without spending thousands?*

---

### Formula 12 — The Statement Hook
A single declarative sentence with quiet power.
She stops because it sounds like a truth she hasn't heard yet.

**Structure:** `[One powerful declarative sentence]`

**Examples:**
- *Softness is not something you outgrow.*
- *The right product doesn't complete you. It honors you.*
- *Beauty is not a performance. It's a private ritual.*
- *Luxury should feel like breathing, not achieving.*

---

## Hook Length by Platform

| Platform | Hook Length | Notes |
|----------|------------|-------|
| TikTok | 1-2 sentences max | First 2 seconds are everything |
| Instagram Reel | 1 sentence on screen | Text overlay must be instant |
| Instagram Caption | First line before "more" | Under 125 characters |
| Email Subject | 6-9 words | Curiosity or identity-driven |
| Ad Primary Text | First sentence | Under 20 words |
| Pinterest | First line of description | Keyword-aware |
| SMS | Entire message IS the hook | Under 160 chars |

---

## Hook Testing Protocol

Test every hook before scaling:

1. Read it out loud — does it sound human?
2. Does it make you feel something in under 5 seconds?
3. Could any other brand have written this? (If yes — rewrite)
4. Is it leading with feeling or information?
5. Would she stop scrolling for this?

Run 2-3 hook variations per piece of content.
Track which hooks drive the most saves, shares, and link clicks.
Build a swipe file of top performers in `13_Research_And_Inspiration/Swipe_Files.md`

---
*MVQUEEN Hook Systems — Operational Document*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Brand_Messaging.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 10331 bytes, 212 lines**
# 👑 MVQUEEN — Brand Messaging
### The Messaging Framework

---

## What This File Is

Brand messaging is not brand voice. Voice is how we sound. Messaging is what we say — the specific, repeatable statements that communicate MVQUEEN's value, position, and identity to different audiences in different contexts.

This file defines the message hierarchy, the core message, supporting messages, audience-specific messaging, and the platform-specific message adaptations that keep MVQUEEN's communication consistent without being repetitive.

Every copywriter, AI agent, and campaign brief pulls from this file when they need to know: *what is the essential thing MVQUEEN says in this context?*

---

## PART 1 — THE MESSAGE HIERARCHY

### Level 01 — The Master Message
*The single most important thing MVQUEEN communicates. Everything else serves this.*

> **Luxury was always yours.**

This is not a slogan. It is a belief that sits underneath everything the brand says. When any message lands correctly, she feels this truth — whether the words say it directly or not.

---

### Level 02 — The Core Brand Message
*The brand in one paragraph. Used in About pages, press kits, investor materials, partnership introductions.*

> MVQUEEN is a modern feminine luxury lifestyle brand built for the woman who has been told — through price, through exclusivity, through the aesthetics of traditional luxury — that elevated, beautiful things weren't meant for her. We were built on the rejection of that idea. Every product, every word, every experience in the MVQUEEN world was designed to make one thing true: that luxury, confidence, and elevation are not something to earn. They were always hers.

---

### Level 03 — The Supporting Messages
*3–5 sentences that reinforce the master message from different angles. Used in campaigns, email, social, and any context where the brand introduces itself.*

**Supporting Message A — The Positioning Message**
> MVQUEEN sits at the intersection of accessible luxury and emotional intention. Not mass-market. Not out of reach. The space between — where the experience is real and the price is attainable.

**Supporting Message B — The Product Message**
> We make fashion, beauty, skincare, fragrance, haircare, and lifestyle products that don't just perform — they feel like something. Because the product is only part of what she's buying. The ritual, the atmosphere, the way it makes her carry herself — that's the rest.

**Supporting Message C — The Identity Message**
> MVQUEEN is for the woman who gets dressed for herself. Who treats her skincare like a ritual. Who chooses her fragrance the way she chooses her words — with intention. She doesn't need to be told she deserves this. She already knows. We just made the world to match.

**Supporting Message D — The Sister Brand Message**
> MVQUEEN and Miss.Princess are sister brands — two distinct worlds built on the same belief. MVQUEEN is the elegance of having arrived. Miss.Princess is the joy of becoming. Together, they cover every woman, every mood, every stage.

**Supporting Message E — The Legacy Message**
> MVQUEEN is not a trend. It is not built for a season or a demographic moment. It is built for the long arc — the brand that becomes part of how a woman thinks about herself, not just what she buys.

---

## PART 2 — AUDIENCE-SPECIFIC MESSAGING

Different audiences need to hear different things first. The truth doesn't change — the entry point does.

### Audience 01 — New Customer (Discovery Stage)
*She has just found MVQUEEN. She doesn't know the brand yet. She needs to feel welcome.*

**Primary message:** *This world was built for you.*

**What she needs to hear:**
- This brand understands women like her
- The products are within reach and worth the investment
- The brand is real — not manufactured aspiration
- She belongs here without having to earn entry

**Key phrases:**
> "Luxury was always yours."
> "Made for the woman who already knows her worth."
> "Not a store. A world — and it was built for you."
> "Accessible luxury. Designed for real life."

---

### Audience 02 — Returning Customer (Loyalty Stage)
*She has purchased before. She came back. She needs to feel recognized.*

**Primary message:** *You're part of something we're building together.*

**What she needs to hear:**
- The brand remembers her and values her return
- New things have been built with her in mind
- Her relationship with MVQUEEN deepens over time
- She is community, not just a customer

**Key phrases:**
> "You came back. We built this for when you did."
> "The next chapter of the world you already live in."
> "For the woman who already knows what MVQUEEN feels like."
> "Welcome back to your world."

---

### Audience 03 — Press / Media
*She is writing about the brand. She needs a clear, compelling, quotable story.*

**Primary message:** *MVQUEEN exists to close the gap between luxury and real women.*

**What she needs to hear:**
- The brand has a clear, distinct positioning in the market
- The founder story is real and specific
- The brand is building something with cultural staying power
- Miss.Princess is a sister brand — two distinct identities, one vision

**Key phrases:**
> "MVQUEEN was built in the space traditional luxury ignores — the woman who wants the experience without being made to feel excluded by the price."
> "We don't compete with heritage luxury. We serve the market they leave behind."
> "Two brands, one belief: every woman deserves to feel like the most valuable version of herself."

---

### Audience 04 — Brand Partners / Collaborators
*She or he is evaluating MVQUEEN as a partner. They need to understand the brand's position and audience clearly.*

**Primary message:** *MVQUEEN is building a loyal community of emotionally intelligent feminine consumers.*

**What they need to hear:**
- Clear audience demographics and psychographics
- Distinct brand identity that doesn't blur in collaboration
- Quality standard that protects partner perception
- Long-term brand vision — not a short-term moment

**Key phrases:**
> "Our audience is the modern feminine woman — emotionally aware, aesthetically driven, and deeply loyal to brands that actually see her."
> "MVQUEEN doesn't dilute in collaboration. We bring a clear identity and a specific audience."
> "We build long-term. Our collaborations are chosen with the same intention as our products."

---

### Audience 05 — Investors / Business Stakeholders
*They are evaluating the commercial opportunity. They need the brand story through a business lens.*

**Primary message:** *MVQUEEN owns a gap in the market that no major brand currently serves with intention.*

**What they need to hear:**
- Clear market positioning
- Dual-brand ecosystem with distinct audiences
- AI-assisted, scalable OS infrastructure
- Long-term brand vision beyond product catalog

**Key phrases:**
> "Traditional luxury serves the top of the market. Mass beauty serves the bottom. MVQUEEN owns the emotionally intelligent middle — accessible luxury with genuine brand depth."
> "We built the brand and the operating system simultaneously — so scale doesn't compromise identity."
> "Miss.Princess extends the ecosystem into a younger, trend-aware demographic without diluting MVQUEEN's positioning."

---

## PART 3 — MESSAGE ADAPTATION BY PLATFORM

The core message stays consistent. The register adapts.

| Platform | Message Register | What Changes |
|---|---|---|
| Website homepage | Cinematic, atmospheric | Full brand world, slow reveal |
| Product page | Sensory, specific | Product-first desire, then identity |
| Email | Personal, warm | Feels like a letter, not a broadcast |
| Instagram feed | Poetic, editorial | Visual carries most of the message |
| TikTok | Direct, real | Conversational, first-person |
| Pinterest | Aspirational, searchable | SEO-forward but brand-voiced |
| SMS | Intimate, brief | Maximum 1 idea, warm CTA |
| Press release | Factual, quotable | Third-person, specific, newsworthy |
| Partnership brief | Professional, positioning-led | Brand metrics + vision |

---

## PART 4 — WHAT MVQUEEN NEVER SAYS

Regardless of context or audience, these messages are never used:

| Message | Why It's Wrong |
|---|---|
| "Empowering women since [year]" | Hollow, overused, generic |
| "Luxury for everyone" | Sounds like discounting, not elevation |
| "We're different from other brands" | Show it, don't say it |
| "Join the movement" | Activist language without activist stakes |
| "You deserve the best" | Generic self-help tone |
| "Quality you can trust" | Corporate platitude |
| "Shop our collection today" | Zero brand voice, sounds like a flyer |
| Any message with "boss babe" or "girl boss" | Expired language — see Forbidden_Words.md |

---

## PART 5 — MISS.PRINCESS MESSAGING

Miss.Princess carries the same master message — *luxury was always yours* — but expresses it through her own register:

**Miss.Princess Core Message:**
> Miss.Princess is for the woman who romanticizes everything — her beauty routine, her aesthetic, her whole soft, sparkling world. This isn't a phase. It's a personality. And it deserves products, fashion, and beauty built specifically for the energy she brings.

**Miss.Princess Supporting Messages:**
- *Pretty is a whole personality. We built a brand around it.*
- *The soft girl aesthetic, elevated. Miss.Princess.*
- *Cute on purpose. Every single day.*
- *For the girl who makes getting ready the best part.*

---

## THE MESSAGING AUDIT TEST

Before any brand communication is published, run it through these three questions:

1. **Does it serve the master message?** Does "luxury was always yours" feel true after reading it?
2. **Is it written for the right audience at the right stage?** Discovery, loyalty, press, partner, investor — is the entry point calibrated?
3. **Does it sound specifically like MVQUEEN?** Could it belong to another brand — or is this unmistakably ours?

All three yes — it publishes.

---

*This file is the MVQUEEN brand messaging framework. It pairs with Brand_Essence.md (what the brand is), USP.md (what makes it different), Example_Copy.md (what the voice looks like in practice), and Writing_Rules.md (how every message is constructed).*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Tone_Guide.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 5005 bytes, 164 lines**
# 👑 MVQUEEN — Tone & Voice System

---

## The Voice of MVQUEEN

MVQUEEN speaks like a woman who has arrived.

Not loudly. Not desperately. Not with urgency or pressure.

She speaks with quiet confidence — the kind that doesn't need to announce itself.
Warm enough to feel human. Elevated enough to feel luxury.
Feminine without being fragile. Aspirational without being distant.

If MVQUEEN were a woman in a room, she would be the one
whose presence you felt before she spoke.

---

## Voice Identity

| Dimension | MVQUEEN Is | MVQUEEN Is Never |
|-----------|-----------|-----------------|
| Tone | Warm, calm, confident | Cold, corporate, aggressive |
| Energy | Soft power, quiet luxury | Loud flex, desperate urgency |
| Intimacy | Personal, emotionally aware | Robotic, transactional |
| Aspiration | Inviting, inclusive | Intimidating, exclusionary |
| Intelligence | Thoughtful, intentional | Performative, shallow |
| Femininity | Grounded, present | Stereotyped, overdone |

---

## The Four Voice Pillars

### 01 — Emotional Warmth
Every piece of communication should make a woman feel seen —
not sold to.
Write as though you know her interior life,
not just her shopping behavior.

### 02 — Quiet Confidence
MVQUEEN does not beg for attention.
It does not chase trends with desperate relevance.
The brand speaks with the certainty of something that knows its worth.
Short sentences. Deliberate words. Confident pauses.

### 03 — Sensory Intelligence
MVQUEEN language should activate the senses —
the way a texture feels, the way light falls soft,
the way a scent lingers in memory.
Write in ways that create atmosphere, not just information.

### 04 — Feminine Precision
Every word is chosen. Nothing is filler.
Luxury is restraint. Apply this to language.
A single precise line carries more weight than three vague ones.

---

## Sentence Architecture

**Short sentences create power.**
Use them for declarations, product names, CTAs, and emotional moments.

*She deserves this.*
*Softness is a standard.*
*Built for women who feel everything.*

**Flowing sentences create atmosphere.**
Use them for brand stories, product descriptions, and emotional narratives.

*MVQUEEN was designed for the woman who moves through life with intention —
who chooses beauty not to perform it, but to live inside it.*

**Lists create clarity.**
Use them sparingly — only when structure serves the reader.
Never use them as a substitute for real writing.

---

## Platform Voice Adaptation

### Product Descriptions
Sensory, aspirational, precise.
Lead with feeling — close with function.
Never list features. Translate them into experiences.

❌ *Moisturizing formula with vitamin E and hyaluronic acid.*
✅ *Skin that drinks it in. The kind of softness you notice by evening.*

### Captions & Social
Intimate. Conversational. Never try-hard.
Write like you're speaking to one woman — not broadcasting to thousands.
End with presence, not pressure.

❌ *Shop now before it sells out!! Link in bio 🛍️*
✅ *For the version of you that already knows she deserves this.*

### Email
Personal. Warm. Paced like a letter — not a flyer.
Open with atmosphere. Close with invitation.
Subject lines should feel like whispers, not headlines.

❌ *SALE ENDS TONIGHT — 40% OFF EVERYTHING*
✅ *Something we made for you.*

### SMS
Brief. Intimate. Never intrusive.
One thought. One feeling. One invitation.

✅ *Your order is on its way. We wrapped it with intention.*

### Ad Copy
Emotionally precise. Identity-driven. Never benefit-feature.
Speak to who she is becoming — not what she is buying.

❌ *High-quality luxury skincare for all skin types.*
✅ *For the woman who treats softness like a discipline.*

---

## Words We Use

*soft, presence, intention, atmosphere, restored, elevated, feminine,
warmth, ritual, grounded, living, breathe, quiet, grace, unhurried,
crafted, human, intelligent, chosen, sacred, slow, becoming*

## Words We Avoid

*amazing, incredible, game-changer, hustle, boss, empowered (overused),
luxury (overused without context), exclusive (without meaning),
emotionally (as a prefix for everything), synergy, optimize (in brand copy)*

---

## The Test

Before publishing any communication, ask:

1. Does this sound like MVQUEEN — or like any other brand?
2. Does this make a woman feel elevated — or pressured?
3. Is every word earning its place?
4. Would this feel at home in a luxury editorial — or a flash sale?

If it fails any of these — rewrite it.

---

## Voice Governance

The Tone & Voice System governs:
- all product copy
- all email and SMS communication
- all social media content
- all ad creative
- all AI-generated content before publication
- all customer service communication
- all campaign messaging

No output leaves MVQUEEN without passing through this system.

---
*MVQUEEN Tone & Voice System — Operational Document*
*All content creators, AI systems, and collaborators must operate within this framework.*

### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Ad_Copy_Voice.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 4503 bytes, 170 lines**
# 📣 MVQUEEN — Ad Copy Voice Guide

---

## Ads Are a First Impression

Most women who see a MVQUEEN ad have never heard of the brand.
In 2-3 seconds, the ad must:
- Stop the scroll
- Create desire or recognition
- Make her want to know more

MVQUEEN ads don't shout. They magnetize.
The goal is never to interrupt — it is to belong in her feed so naturally
that she stops because she wants to, not because she had to.

---

## Ad Voice Principles

**1. Hook is everything**
The first line, first frame, or first visual must earn the next second.
If it doesn't stop her, nothing else matters.

**2. Emotion before information**
She feels it before she reads it. The feeling is the message.
Features and details come after — if at all.

**3. Identity over urgency**
She buys because of who she is, not because of how little time she has.
Speak to her identity. Never to her fear.

**4. Specificity creates trust**
Vague claims are invisible. Specific details are magnetic.
Not "amazing results" — "skin that glows before she puts makeup on."

**5. One message per ad**
One feeling. One product. One action.
The ad that tries to say everything says nothing.

---

## Ad Formats and Voice by Type

### Static Image Ad (Facebook / Instagram)

**Headline formula:**
```
[Identity statement OR sensory detail OR bold truth]
```

**Examples:**
- She built her glow from the inside out.
- Two drops. That's the whole routine.
- The kind of skin that makes her feel like herself again.
- Soft. Intentional. Unmistakably hers.
- She doesn't explain her glow. She just has it.

**Body copy formula:**
```
[Expand the feeling — 1-2 sentences]
[Product name + what it does in emotional language]
[Soft CTA]
```

**Example:**
```
She doesn't follow trends. She sets her own ritual.
MVQUEEN Luminous Face Oil — 3 drops, every morning, no exceptions.
Make it yours →
```

---

### Video / Reel Ad (15-30 seconds)

**Hook (0-3 seconds):**
Visual or audio that creates immediate recognition or desire.
Must work on mute AND with sound.

**Hook examples:**
- [Visual: her morning ritual, slow motion, warm light] + text: "Her secret isn't a product."
- [Product reveal] + voiceover: "She's been asked about her skin every day this week."
- [Close-up texture] + text: "Two drops changed her whole morning."

**Middle (3-20 seconds):**
Show the product in context — her world, her ritual, her result.
Not a clinical demo. A feeling.

**Close (last 5 seconds):**
Brand name + product name + CTA.
Simple. Clean. Confident.

---

### Carousel Ad

Each slide carries a single idea. Together they tell one story.

**Carousel flow example:**
- Slide 1: The hook — emotion or bold statement
- Slide 2: The ritual — how she uses it
- Slide 3: The result — what she feels
- Slide 4: The product — clean reveal
- Slide 5: The CTA — "Shop the collection"

---

### Retargeting Ad

She's seen MVQUEEN before. This ad reminds her why she stopped.

**Tone:** Softer. More personal. Assumes familiarity.

**Examples:**
```
She was looking at this for a reason.
[Product name] — still here when she's ready. →
```

```
Some decisions take a moment.
She's had her moment. The collection is waiting. 👑
```

---

## Headline Swipe File (Tested Formats)

**Identity-based:**
- She built her ritual around this.
- For the woman who takes her time.
- The glow she stopped trying to explain.
- Made for her kind of morning.
- Not every woman gets it. She does.

**Sensory-based:**
- Skin so soft she'll keep touching it.
- A scent she'll name her mood after.
- The finish that catches light like nothing else.
- Weightless. Luminous. Unmistakably her.

**Curiosity-based:**
- She changed one thing in her routine. Everything followed.
- The product her friends keep asking about.
- What her skin looks like before makeup.
- She almost didn't share this one.

**Product truth:**
- Two drops. Every morning. That's the ritual.
- [Product name] — the one she reaches for first.
- Her skin is doing the most. The secret: [product name].

---

## Ad Copy Never Includes

- Exclamation marks in headlines (they signal cheap urgency)
- "Limited time" language on standard ads
- Before/after with shame-based before
- Claims that can't be substantiated
- Competitor comparisons
- Generic beauty category language ("glowing skin," "beautiful you")
- All caps in body copy
- More than one CTA

---

*06_Tone_And_Voice / Ad_Copy_Voice.md*
*The best MVQUEEN ad doesn't feel like an ad. It feels like something she found.*


---
### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Email_Voice.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 5333 bytes, 167 lines**
# 📧 MVQUEEN — Email Voice Guide

---

## How MVQUEEN Sounds in Email

Email is the most intimate channel MVQUEEN has.
It lands in her personal space — not her feed, not a search result.
Her inbox. That's a privilege.

MVQUEEN email voice honors that privilege by sounding like a message from someone who knows her — not a campaign from a company that wants her money.

The goal of every email: make her feel something before she clicks anything.

---

## Email Voice Dimensions

| Element | MVQUEEN Email | Never |
|---------|--------------|-------|
| Opening | Personal, scene-setting, emotionally grounded | "We're excited to share..." |
| Tone | Warm, intimate, woman-to-woman | Corporate, promotional, pressured |
| Length | Right-sized for the purpose — never padded | Long for the sake of appearing thorough |
| Subject line | Intriguing, identity-based, or emotionally specific | "SALE — 30% off everything!!!" |
| CTA | Soft, inviting, one per email | Multiple competing CTAs |
| Closing | Warm, signature-feel | "The MVQUEEN Team" (cold) |

---

## Subject Line Formulas

**Identity-based (she sees herself)**
- The woman who takes her time →
- She built her morning around this.
- Not every woman will get it. She will.
- For the one who chooses herself first.

**Curiosity-based (she needs to open)**
- Something changed in her routine this week.
- She almost didn't share this one.
- The product she keeps going back to.
- We made something for her quiet hours.

**Occasion-based (specific moment)**
- Her Friday ritual starts here.
- Sunday was made for this.
- A gift she didn't know she needed.

**Product/launch-based (direct with texture)**
- [Product Name] — finally here.
- The collection she's been waiting for.
- New. And it's everything we hoped for.
- She asked for this. We listened.

**Re-engagement (soft, personal)**
- She's been on our mind.
- Something new just arrived — we thought of her.
- It's been a moment. Here's what she missed.

---

## Preview Text Principles

Preview text should complement the subject — never repeat it.
If the subject creates intrigue, preview text adds warmth.
If the subject is direct, preview text adds texture.

**Examples:**
- Subject: "The collection she's been waiting for."
  Preview: "Built for her rituals. Available now."

- Subject: "Something changed in her routine this week."
  Preview: "Two drops. That's all it took."

- Subject: "For the one who chooses herself first."
  Preview: "A ritual designed around her, not her schedule."

---

## Email Opening Lines (by type)

**Welcome email**
- She made a decision today — and it suits her.
- Something is different about this place. She'll feel it.
- MVQUEEN was built for a woman like her.

**Product launch**
- This one has been in development for a while. She was worth the wait.
- She asked for something that felt like [emotion]. Here it is.
- New to the collection — and already a ritual staple.

**Promotional**
- This is not a sale email. It's an invitation.
- The collection is available — at a price that makes sense right now.
- A moment to shop what she's been saving.

**Content / editorial**
- She started her morning differently last week. This is why.
- There is a way to [outcome]. She found it.
- Some rituals take five minutes. Some change the whole day.

**Re-engagement / winback**
- It's been a little while. Things have changed here — beautifully.
- She doesn't need a reason to come back. But we have one anyway.
- Something new just arrived. We thought of her immediately.

---

## Body Copy Rules

**Rule 1 — One message per email**
Every email has one emotional purpose and one primary CTA.
Not three products and four links and two banners. One thing. Done beautifully.

**Rule 2 — Short paragraphs**
Two to three sentences maximum per paragraph. She's reading on her phone.
White space is not wasted — it lets the copy breathe.

**Rule 3 — Lead with feeling, end with product**
She should feel something in the first two lines before she sees a product name.

**Rule 4 — No exclamation marks in body copy**
The voice is warm — not excitable. Enthusiasm shows in word choice, not punctuation.
Exception: SMS only, and even then, sparingly.

**Rule 5 — She, not you**
MVQUEEN email often refers to the customer in third person ("she") in narrative passages
before shifting to second person ("you") for direct address.
This creates a mirror effect — she sees a woman she recognizes.

---

## Signature Closings

**Standard:**
With warmth,
MVQUEEN 👑

**Personal / campaign:**
Made with her in mind,
MVQUEEN

**Seasonal:**
With love this [season],
MVQUEEN

**Launch:**
She waited long enough.
MVQUEEN 👑

---

## What Never Appears in MVQUEEN Email

- "We're excited to announce" — start with the thing
- Excessive emoji use — one maximum, and only if it fits naturally
- Countdown timers on regular sends — reserved for specific drops only
- Guilt-based re-engagement language ("You haven't shopped in a while...")
- Generic social proof ("Join thousands of happy customers") — be specific or omit
- More than one CTA button per email — choose one
- ALL CAPS anywhere in body copy
- Excessive exclamation marks — never in body copy

---

*06_Tone_And_Voice / Email_Voice.md*
*Her inbox is a privilege. Write accordingly.*

### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/Social_Voice.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 4105 bytes, 129 lines**
# 🗣️ MVQUEEN — Social Voice Guide

---

## Purpose

Define exactly how MVQUEEN speaks on every social platform — with real examples of right and wrong, platform-specific adaptations, and a voice test to apply before every post.

---

## The Social Voice Identity

MVQUEEN on social sounds like a woman who has arrived — quietly, confidently, without announcement. She doesn't perform for the algorithm. She creates for the woman she's speaking to.

**In one sentence:** Warm enough to feel human. Elevated enough to feel luxury. Real enough to feel true.

---

## Voice Dimensions on Social

| Dimension | Standard | Never |
|-----------|---------|-------|
| Intimacy | Speaks to one woman, not thousands | Broadcast announcements |
| Confidence | States things — doesn't hedge or over-explain | Self-deprecation, apologetic tone |
| Warmth | Feels like someone who knows you | Cold brand speak, corporate tone |
| Intelligence | Trusts her intelligence | Oversimplification, patronizing |
| Aspiration | Invites her into something better | Pressure, comparison, inadequacy |

---

## Instagram Voice

### Feed Posts
**Tone:** Aspirational, intimate, visually supported
**Length:** 80-150 words for narrative posts, under 50 for atmosphere posts
**Opening:** Must work as a standalone sentence — hooks before the "more" cut

**Right:**
*The ritual that changed my mornings wasn't complicated.*
*It was intentional.*
*[Product Name] — link in bio.*

**Wrong:**
*Hey girlies!! This product is literally SO AMAZING you guys need to try it ASAP!! Shop the link in bio before it sells out!! 🛍️🔥*

### Reels Captions
**Tone:** Conversational, real, slightly more casual than feed
**Length:** Under 80 words
**Opening:** Continues or expands the video hook

### Stories
**Tone:** Most casual format — behind the scenes, real moments, interactive
**Length:** Single thought per frame
**Voice:** Like texting a friend who has great taste

---

## TikTok Voice

TikTok demands realness. Less polish, more truth.

**Right:**
*Nobody talks about how skincare routines are supposed to restore you — not add to your to-do list. Here's what changed for me...*

**Wrong:**
*Hi everyone! Today I'm going to be showing you this amazing luxury skincare product from MVQUEEN that has completely transformed my skin!*

**Rules:**
- Speak naturally — no script-reading cadence
- Say the keyword out loud in the video (TikTok transcribes)
- End with a soft invite, never a hard sell
- Comment back on every comment in the first hour

---

## Pinterest Voice

Pinterest is search. Write for the woman who is actively looking.

**Right:**
*Luxury face serum for women who want their morning ritual to feel intentional. Lightweight, absorbs instantly, stays soft all day. Part of the MVQUEEN ritual.*

**Wrong:**
*OMG this serum is everything!! So obsessed with how my skin looks!*

**Rules:**
- First sentence contains primary keyword
- Descriptive and atmospheric
- 100-150 words for maximum reach
- Hashtags at end: 3-5 relevant, not excessive

---

## Facebook Voice

Facebook skews slightly older, more conversational, community-first.

**Right:**
*For the women in this community — what does your evening ritual look like? We're always curious what the women who find MVQUEEN are already doing before they find us.*

**Wrong:**
*SHOP NOW! New arrivals just dropped and they're going fast!!*

**Rules:**
- Community questions drive engagement better than announcements
- Longer captions acceptable — Facebook reads them
- Repurpose Instagram content but adapt the opening line

---

## Voice Test (Apply Before Every Post)

```
□ Does this sound like MVQUEEN — or like any other brand?
□ Does it speak to one woman — not an audience?
□ Is the first line strong enough to stand alone?
□ Is every word earning its place?
□ Does it make her feel elevated — not pressured?
□ Would she save or share this?
□ Does it pass the forbidden words check?
```

If any box is unchecked — rewrite before posting.

---
*MVQUEEN Social Voice Guide — Operational Document*

---
---
---

### FILE: 06_Tone_And_Voice/SMS_Voice.md
**STATUS: REBUILT — 2814 bytes, 114 lines**
# 📱 MVQUEEN — SMS Voice Guide

---

## SMS Is Different

SMS is the most direct channel MVQUEEN has.
No algorithm. No competition for attention. It lands on her lock screen.

That means two things:
1. It must earn its place — never feel spammy or frivolous
2. It must be immediately valuable, beautiful, or both

MVQUEEN SMS is short, warm, specific, and personal.
It sounds like a message from a brand she loves — not a brand that bought her number.

---

## SMS Voice Rules

**Rule 1 — Under 160 characters when possible**
She reads it in one glance. Make that glance count.

**Rule 2 — Lead with the value**
She sees the first 40 characters before she decides to open. Start with what matters.

**Rule 3 — One message, one action**
One reason to text. One link. One thing she can do.

**Rule 4 — Warm but efficient**
Not cold. Not robotic. But also not padded. Say it in her language, then stop.

**Rule 5 — Never pressure**
No countdown clocks in SMS. No "HURRY." No "LAST CHANCE" in all caps.
Urgency through tone, never through panic.

---

## SMS Templates by Type

### Welcome (first message after opt-in)
```
👑 Welcome to MVQUEEN. You're in her world now.
Explore the collection: [link]
```

### Product Launch
```
She's been waiting. [Product Name] is live. ✨
[link]
```

### Promotional
```
MVQUEEN: The collection — available at [offer] through [date].
Made for her: [link]
```

### Back in Stock
```
[Product Name] is back. 👑
It went fast last time. Yours: [link]
```

### Loyalty / VIP
```
Queen — your rewards are waiting.
[X] points = [Y reward]. Redeem: [link] 👑
```

### Abandoned Cart Recovery
```
She left something behind. ✨
Still yours if she wants it: [link]
```

### Post-Purchase
```
Her order is on its way. 👑
[Product Name] ships [date]. Track it: [link]
```

### Re-engagement
```
MVQUEEN: Something new just arrived — we thought of her.
[link]
```

---

## What MVQUEEN Never Sends via SMS

- Mass blasts with no personalization signal
- More than 4 SMS per month (unless VIP tier with explicit preference)
- Urgency language in all caps
- Multiple links
- Anything that could have been an email — SMS is reserved for high-value, time-sensitive moments
- Generic promotional language ("Sale ends soon!!!")

---

## Tone Comparison

| Generic Brand SMS | MVQUEEN SMS |
|------------------|-------------|
| SALE! 30% OFF EVERYTHING! Shop now → | The collection — thoughtfully priced this week. Yours: [link] |
| Last chance! Don't miss out! | She won't want to miss this one. [link] 👑 |
| Hi [NAME], we miss you! Come back! | Something new just arrived. We thought of her: [link] |
| Your cart is waiting! | She left something. Still yours: [link] ✨ |

---

*06_Tone_And_Voice / SMS_Voice.md*
*Her lock screen is sacred. Be worth it.*
